[40m[37m   1:[49m[39m # This file is used to manage the dependencies of the Chromium src repo. It is
[40m[37m   2:[49m[39m # used by gclient to determine what version of each dependency to check out, and
[40m[37m   3:[49m[39m # where.
[40m[37m   4:[49m[39m #
[40m[37m   5:[49m[39m # For more information, please refer to the official documentation:
[40m[37m   6:[49m[39m #   https://sites.google.com/a/chromium.org/dev/developers/how-tos/get-the-code
[40m[37m   7:[49m[39m #
[40m[37m   8:[49m[39m # When adding a new dependency, please update the top-level .gitignore file
[40m[37m   9:[49m[39m # to list the dependency's destination directory.
[40m[37m  10:[49m[39m #
[40m[37m  11:[49m[39m # -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
[40m[37m  12:[49m[39m # Rolling deps
[40m[37m  13:[49m[39m # -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
[40m[37m  14:[49m[39m # All repositories in this file are git-based, using Chromium git mirrors where
[40m[37m  15:[49m[39m # necessary (e.g., a git mirror is used when the source project is SVN-based).
[40m[37m  16:[49m[39m # To update the revision that Chromium pulls for a given dependency:
[40m[37m  17:[49m[39m #
[40m[37m  18:[49m[39m #  # Create and switch to a new branch
[40m[37m  19:[49m[39m #  git new-branch depsroll
[40m[37m  20:[49m[39m #  # Run roll-dep (provided by depot_tools) giving the dep's path and optionally
[40m[37m  21:[49m[39m #  # a regex that will match the line in this file that contains the current
[40m[37m  22:[49m[39m #  # revision. The script ALWAYS rolls the dependency to the latest revision
[40m[37m  23:[49m[39m #  # in origin/master. The path for the dep should start with src/.
[40m[37m  24:[49m[39m #  roll-dep src/third_party/foo_package/src foo_package.git
[40m[37m  25:[49m[39m #  # You should now have a modified DEPS file; commit and upload as normal
[40m[37m  26:[49m[39m #  git commit -aspv_he
[40m[37m  27:[49m[39m #  git cl upload
[40m[37m  28:[49m[39m #
[40m[37m  29:[49m[39m # For more on the syntax and semantics of this file, see:
[40m[37m  30:[49m[39m #   https://bit.ly/chromium-gclient-conditionals
[40m[37m  31:[49m[39m #
[40m[37m  32:[49m[39m # which is a bit incomplete but the best documentation we have at the
[40m[37m  33:[49m[39m # moment.
[40m[37m  34:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  35:[49m[39m # We expect all git dependencies specified in this file to be in sync with git
[40m[37m  36:[49m[39m # submodules (gitlinks).
[40m[37m  37:[49m[39m git_dependencies = 'SYNC'
[40m[37m  38:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  39:[49m[39m gclient_gn_args_file = 'src/build/config/gclient_args.gni'
[40m[37m  40:[49m[39m gclient_gn_args = [
[40m[37m  41:[49m[39m   'build_with_chromium',
[40m[37m  42:[49m[39m   'checkout_android',
[40m[37m  43:[49m[39m   'checkout_android_prebuilts_build_tools',
[40m[37m  44:[49m[39m   'checkout_clang_coverage_tools',
[40m[37m  45:[49m[39m   'checkout_copybara',
[40m[37m  46:[49m[39m   'checkout_glic_e2e_tests',
[40m[37m  47:[49m[39m   'checkout_ios_webkit',
[40m[37m  48:[49m[39m   'checkout_mutter',
[40m[37m  49:[49m[39m   'checkout_openxr',
[40m[37m  50:[49m[39m   'checkout_src_internal',
[40m[37m  51:[49m[39m   'checkout_src_internal_infra',
[40m[37m  52:[49m[39m   'cros_boards',
[40m[37m  53:[49m[39m   'cros_boards_with_qemu_images',
[40m[37m  54:[49m[39m   'generate_location_tags',
[40m[37m  55:[49m[39m ]
[40m[37m  56:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  57:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  58:[49m[39m vars = {
[40m[37m  59:[49m[39m   # Variable that can be used to support multiple build scenarios, like having
[40m[37m  60:[49m[39m   # Chromium specific targets in a client project's GN file or sync dependencies
[40m[37m  61:[49m[39m   # conditionally etc.
[40m[37m  62:[49m[39m   'build_with_chromium': True,
[40m[37m  63:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  64:[49m[39m   # By default, we should check out everything needed to run on the main
[40m[37m  65:[49m[39m   # chromium waterfalls. This var can be also be set to "small", in order
[40m[37m  66:[49m[39m   # to skip things are not strictly needed to build chromium for development
[40m[37m  67:[49m[39m   # purposes, by adding the following line to src.git's .gclient entry:
[40m[37m  68:[49m[39m   #      "custom_vars": { "checkout_configuration": "small" },
[40m[37m  69:[49m[39m   'checkout_configuration': 'default',
[40m[37m  70:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  71:[49m[39m   # By default, don't check out android. Will be overridden by gclient
[40m[37m  72:[49m[39m   # variables.
[40m[37m  73:[49m[39m   # TODO(crbug.com/875037): Remove this once the problem in gclient is fixed.
[40m[37m  74:[49m[39m   'checkout_android': False,
[40m[37m  75:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  76:[49m[39m   # By default, don't check out Fuchsia. Will be overridden by gclient

[40m[37m  80:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m  81:[49m[39m   # For code related to internal Fuchsia images.
[40m[37m  82:[49m[39m   'checkout_fuchsia_internal': False,
[40m[37m  83:[49m[39m

[40m[37m  85:[49m[39m   # comma-separated list.

[40m[37m 108:[49m[39m

[40m[37m 111:[49m[39m 
[40m[37m 112:[49m[39m   # By default, checkout JavaScript coverage node modules. These packages

[40m[37m 114:[49m[39m   # output.
[40m[37m 115:[49m[39m   'checkout_js_coverage_modules': True,

[40m[37m 126:[49m[39m   # custom_vars. This acts the same way as checkout_src_internal, but only affects
